    <section class="core-section-container
        core-section-container--with-border border-b-1 border-solid border-color-border-faint py-4 text-color-text" data-test-id="about-us">
<!---->
          <h2 class="core-section-container__title section-title">
            Hakkımızda
          </h2>

<!---->
      <div class="core-section-container__content break-words">
        

          <p class="break-words text-color-text" data-test-id="about-us__description">
              BilgeAdam Teknoloji, 1.800'den fazla profesyonelden oluşan ekibi ile global bir yazılım ve teknoloji hizmetleri şirketidir.
Yazılım geliştirme, kalite mühendisliği ve teknoloji servislerinde 25 yılı aşkın deneyim sahibi olan BilgeAadam Teknoloji, mühendislik becerileri ve sektör bilgisini bir arada kullanarak, müşterilerinin başarıya ulaşmalarına yardımcı olur.
BilgeAdam Teknoloji; yurt içinde İstanbul ve Ankara’daki teknokent ofislerinde hizmet vermektedir. Global operasyonlarını ise Londra ve Sheffield – İngiltere, Den Haag – Hollanda ve Düsseldorf – Almanya’daki ofisleriyle yürütmektedir.
Müşterilerine kaliteli, verimli, yenilikçi ve sonuç odaklı hizmetler sunarak katma değer yaratmayı ilke edinen BilgeAdam Teknoloji, 15 uluslararası ödül sahibidir ve Bilişim 500 araştırmasına göre Türkiye’nin en büyük bağımsız yazılım şirketlerinden biridir.

BilgeAdam Technologies is a global software and technology services company with a team of 1,800+ employees. 
With over 25 years of experience in software development, quality engineering, and technology services, we help our customers succeed using a combination of engineering skills and industry knowledge.
BilgeAdam’s engineering centres in Turkey and group companies in London, Den Haag, Düsseldorf, and Istanbul ensure flexibility, velocity, and convenience in delivering tailored solutions to our clients worldwide.
BilgeAdam Technologies prioritises creating added value for enterprises by offering quality, efficient, innovative, and result-oriented services. The company has received 15 international awards and is recognised as one of Turkey's largest independent software companies, according to Bilişim 500 research.
          </p>

    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">IFINTEC 2025’te Platinum Sponsor olarak yerimizi aldık.

Finans teknolojileri alanında sektör profesyonellerini bir araya getiren bu önemli etkinlikte, dönüşümü hızlandıran vizyonumuzu ve teknoloji gücümüzü paylaşma fırsatı bulduk.

Konferans boyunca uzmanlarımız; bankacılıkta domain bazlı yaklaşımın rolü ve yazılım yaşam döngüsünde yapay zeka ile verimliliğin artırılması gibi konularda sektöre ışık tuttular.

BilgeAdam Teknoloji olarak, finans sektöründe inovasyonu ileriye taşımaya ve sürdürülebilir değer yaratmaya devam ediyoruz.

<a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Fbilgeadamteknoloji&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#BilgeAdamTeknoloji</a> <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Fifintec2025&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#IFINTEC2025</a></p>

  <div class="attributed-text-segment-list__container relative mt-1 mb-1.5 babybear:mt-0 babybear:mb-0.5">
    <p class="attributed-text-segment-list__content text-color-text !text-sm whitespace-pre-wrap break-words
        " dir="ltr" data-test-id="main-feed-activity-card__commentary">Today, I had the opportunity to attend the webinar on “<a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Fautomation&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#Automation</a> and <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Fartificialintelligence&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#ArtificialIntelligence</a> in <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Fit&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#IT</a> Operations”, delivered by Mr. <a class="link" href="https://tr.linkedin.com/in/mustafakasikci?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>Mustafa Kaşıkçı</a> under the roof of <a class="link" href="https://tr.linkedin.com/company/bilgeadam?trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>BilgeAdam Teknoloji</a>. I would like to share with you the key insights I gained from this valuable session.

In today’s world, it is a fact that the massive flow of data and the thousands of red alerts triggered by system failures cannot be managed solely by human effort. At this point, automation and artificial intelligence have become the preferred solutions for large, corporate organizations that aim to expand their business in line with the requirements of the digital age. Artificial intelligence, through algorithms integrated into a company’s infrastructure, can quickly detect failures and areas requiring maintenance—and even resolve some of these issues automatically. Furthermore, these incidents and insights are visualized through detailed graphics and presented in a clear manner to both IT teams and customers. This enables IT departments to operate faster, work more efficiently, and keep customers fully informed with transparent, data-driven insights.

I was particularly impressed by BilgeAdam’s proprietary automation software. It generates comprehensive reports for each metric, avoids unnecessary complexity, and presents the results through strong and effective visualizations.

In summary, it was a highly valuable webinar, and I extend my sincere thanks to BilgeAdam. I truly believe that every new learning opportunity forms a strong foundation for my professional journey. With this in mind, I look forward to continuing to invest in my own growth and to applying these experiences in future projects that create meaningful value.

<a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Fsoftware&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#Software</a> <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Fartificialintelligence&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#ArtificialIntelligence</a> <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Fautomation&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#Automation</a> <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Fit&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#IT</a> <a class="link" href="https://www.linkedin.com/signup/cold-join?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.linkedin.com%2Ffeed%2Fhashtag%2Fwebinar&amp;_l=tr&amp;trk=organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" target="_self" data-tracking-control-name="organization_guest_main-feed-card-text" data-tracking-will-navigate>#Webinar</a></p>
